The `number of followers` of users in Lithuania on `2023/9/19 7:35 AM UTC`. This list contains users from `Lithuania` and cities `Vilnius` `Kaunas` `Klaipƒóda` `Siauliai` `Panevƒó≈æys` `Alytus`.

There are `138 countries` and `674 cities` can be found [here](https://github.com/isyuricunha/top-github-users).

There are `1625 users`  in Lithuania. You need at least `8 followers` to be on this list.

## üì¶ Third party

- [@octokit/graphql](https://www.npmjs.com/package/@octokit/graphql) - Send GraphQL requests to GitHub API.
- [fs-extra](https://www.npmjs.com/package/fs-extra) - Creating directories and files.
- [simple-git](https://www.npmjs.com/package/simple-git) - Handling Git commands.
